The owners of the inactive mining wallets can opt out by activating their wallets at anytime before the end of the voting that will start on February 21, 2023. The full list of inactive mining wallets can be found here: https://tontech.io/stats/early-miners.
Wallets that did not receive Toncoin directly from the mining smart contracts ("Givers") or made an outgoing transaction at any time in the past will not be affected.

GOSH is a project that aims to promote decentralized science (DeSci) to make scientific research more equitable, thorough, and immune to injustices that many scientists face on a regular basis. DeSci is a researcher-led movement that aims to democratize scientific study for the public good by redefining practices, reinforcing standards, and discovering new paths for the evolution of scientific thought. The article mentions Jocelyn, a decentralized science project named in honor of Jocelyn Bell Burnell, who discovered the radio pulsar but was omitted from the Nobel Prize for her own discovery. Jocelyn is an example of a DeSci project that aims to address some of the issues facing scientists, such as the research replication crisis, difficulty finding funding, and censorship. Therefore, GOSH is relevant to the article because it is a project that is working towards the same goal of promoting DeSci and addressing these issues in scientific research.
